Up until now, Austin vs. McMahon has been the greatest storyline imo. This being because all the greatest storylines touch on angles that are universally relatable.  With Austin and McMahon, the low blue collar rebelling against the corporate tyrant struck a profound chord with the people. We all universally identified with it and lived vicariously through Austin. Just as, if not moreso universal, is the liberation of breaking away from chains from the hold of an abusive person in your life. Every WWE fan who's had to live through that personally no doubt felt this moment and Jimmy's scream in the depths of their soul. The Austin v McMahon story no longer stands alone.
